<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:radiator.html>radiator</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:radiators.html>radiators</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:radiatoren.html>radiatoren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:radiator.html>radiatortje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***radijs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:radijs.html>radijs</a> (40282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:radijs.html>radijs</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">radish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">radis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">radice</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rādīx</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">root; radish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="itc-pro">*wrādīks</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wréh₂ds</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ravel.html>ravel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rafel.html>rafel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rafel.html>rafels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rafel.html>rafeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>frayed thread</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rafelen.html>rafelen</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">rafle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a type game played with three dice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">rafle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">raffle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dice game, <a href = vnd.unilang:plundering.html>plundering</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">rafler</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to snatch, seize, carry off</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">*raffalon</i>, a frequentative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">*raffon</i> (modern German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">raffen</i>). Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rapen.html>rapen</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">raffle</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rafel.html>rafel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rafel.html>rafels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rafel.html>rafeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> type of game played with three dice</li>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">raag</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bol.html>bol</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A brush whose bristly hairs form a curved surface, mounted on a broomstick, mostly used for removing cobwebs. <span class="defdate">[from late 17th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1698</b>, Salomon <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Rusting, "<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kat.html>Kat</a> in '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vagevuur.html>Vagevuur</a>, of Mislyke Kattendroom", in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> vol-geestige <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Salomon <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Ruſting</i>, part 2, Jan ten <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>Hoorn</a> (publ.), page 126.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> ſtaart wiert <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> kannewaſſer, / <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijf.html>lijf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ragebol.html>ragebol</a></b>, / So ruyg, <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> hondert duſent vreſen;</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My tail became like a dish-washing brush, / And my body like a <b>bristly brush</b>, / So rough, because of a hundred thousand fears;</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">halfmaan</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">koppenjager</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kopstubber</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">spinnejager</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***raggen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:raggen.html>raggen</a> (80169)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raggen.html>raggen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move back and forth repeatedly wildly; to wipe, swing or brush wildly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drive recklessly and aggressively
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">rauzen</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***raging.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:raging.html>raging</a> (100813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:raging.html>raging</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rage</i></span></span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1892</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_Besant" class="extiw" title="w:Walter Besant"><a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Besant</a>,  “Prologue: Who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Edmund Gray?”, in  <cite>The Ivory Gate: A Novel</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harper_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Harper (publisher)">Harper amp; Brothers</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Franklin Square">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/16832619">16832619</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/ivorygatenovel00besapage/16/mode/1up">page 16</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Athelstan Arundel walked home all the way, foaming and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:raging.html>raging</a></b>. No omnibus, cab, or conveyance ever built could contain a young <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> in such a rage. His mother lived at Pembridge Square, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> four good measured <a href = vnd.unilang:miles.html>miles</a> from Lincoln's Inn.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:raging.html>raging</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:raging.html>raging</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:raging.html>raging</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Volatile, very active or unpredictable.
<dl><dd><i>A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:raging.html>raging</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>storm</a> kept us indoors.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a person</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In a state of rage; in a state of extreme, often uncontrollable, anger.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:raging.html>raging</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ragings</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A display of rage.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Patrick Brontë and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>To quell the <b>ragings</b> of his Father's ire, / And save a guilty world from quenchless fire!</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rak.html>rak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rak.html>rakken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rak.html>rakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***rakel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rakel.html>rakel</a> (100805)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">rakelen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raken.html>raken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to touch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:raket.html>raket</a> (3531)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Rakete</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">rocchetta</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">rochetto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rocket</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a bobbin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">rocca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a distaff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of Germanic origin, perhaps <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="got">rukka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rukkô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a distaff, a staff with flax fibres tied loosely to it, used in spinning thread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:rocco.html>rocco</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:rocko.html>rocko</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">roccho</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">rocho</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"a distaff"; gt; <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:rocken.html>Rocken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a distaff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">rock</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a distaff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">rokkur</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a distaff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">rocke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a distaff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <i>rock</i>⁴.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">roquette</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">ruchetta</i>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">ruca</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">eruca</i>. Cognate to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">arugula</i>.
</p>

***ramen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ramen.html>ramen</a> (2800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ramen.html>ramen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to aim, to strive for, to guess</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rāmon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rēmijaną</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rēmāną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ramen.html>ramen</a></strong>
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fix an estimate, to budget
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> project <a href = vnd.unilang:kost.html>kost</a> 6 <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:geraamd.html>geraamd</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to guess, to reckon, to deduce</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take aim (at), to watch, to observe</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hit</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tie a bird's wings together to prevent it flying away</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shake

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be shaky, to be incoherent</li></ol>

***rammen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rammen.html>rammen</a> (6962)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rammen.html>rammen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To ram, to intentionally collide with (a ship or car or building) with the intention of damaging or sinking it.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To strike (something) hard.
<dl><dd><i>After placing the cartridge in the <a href = vnd.unilang:musket.html>musket</a>, ram it down securely with the <a href = vnd.unilang:ramrod.html>ramrod</a>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ramp.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ramp.html>ramp</a> (2291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ramp.html>ramp</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">misfortune</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rimpel.html>rimpel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wrinkle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. In the 19th century, the grammatical gender of the word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a matter of debate. It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> finally standardized as feminine, departing from its historical masculine gender.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ramp.html>ramp</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rampen.html>rampen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ramp.html>rampje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">disaster</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">catastrophe</span>
<ul><li><dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>Mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wensen.html>wensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geluk.html>geluk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:welvaart.html>welvaart</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verafschuwen.html>verafschuwen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeluk.html>ongeluk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rampen.html>rampen</a></b>
<dl><dd>People wish happiness and prosperity and abhor mishap and <b>disasters</b></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>an <span class="Latn" lang="en">accident</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:catastrofe.html>catastrofe</a></span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">rampe</i>, back-formation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">ramper</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*rampōn</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*hrampōn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to contract oneself</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***rampart.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rampart.html>rampart</a> (59493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">rempart</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href = vnd.unilang:rampart.html>rampart</a> of a fort</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">remparer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to defend, fortify, inclose with a <a href = vnd.unilang:rampart.html>rampart</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">re-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">again</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">emparer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to defend, fortify, surround, seize, take possesion of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">en-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">parer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to defend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rampart.html>rampart</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ramparts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A defensive mound of earth or a wall with a broad top and usually a stone parapet; a wall-like ridge of earth, stones or debris; an embankment for defensive purpose.</li>
<li>A defensive structure; a protective barrier; a bulwark.</li>
<li>That which defends against intrusion from outside; a protection.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A steep bank of a river or gorge.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rampart.html>rampart</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">ramparts</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ramparting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ramparted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To defend with a <a href = vnd.unilang:rampart.html>rampart</a>; fortify or surround with a <a href = vnd.unilang:rampart.html>rampart</a>.
<ul><li><b>1793</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuel_Taylor_Coleridge" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Samuel Taylor Coleridge">Samuel <a href = vnd.unilang:taylor.html>Taylor</a> Coleridge</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ode.html>Ode</a> on the Departing Year</i>
<dl><dd>Those grassy hills, those glittering dells, / Proudly <b>ramparted</b> with rocks.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">ramparted</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">fraise</span></li></ul>
</body>

***rancor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rancor.html>rancor</a> (100786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in the 13th century as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">rancour</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:rancor.html>rancor</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:rancor.html>rancor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rancidity, grudge, <a href = vnd.unilang:rancor.html>rancor</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*ranceō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">be <a href = vnd.unilang:rotten.html>rotten</a> or putrid, <a href = vnd.unilang:stink.html>stink</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from which also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rancid</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rancor.html>rancor</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">rancors</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_and_British_English_spelling_differences" class="extiw" title="w:American and British English spelling differences">American spelling</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The deepest malignity or spite; deep-seated enmity or malice; inveterate hatred.
<dl><dd><i>I could almost see the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rancor.html>rancor</a></b> in his <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> when he challenged <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to a fight.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***randy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:randy.html>randy</a> (5722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1690, from Scottish <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:randy.html>randy</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boisterous, aggressive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin. Probably from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rand.html>rand</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>storm</a>, rave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">verb</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rant</i>, see <span class="Latn" lang="en">rant</span>; or from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rand.html>rand</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">edge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">noun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, in the sense of "edgy, on edge", from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:rand.html>rand</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">edge, brink, margin, border</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:rand.html>rand</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">edge, border, margin, rim</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="Latn" lang="en">randan</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:randy.html>randy</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">randier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">randiest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Sexually aroused; full of sexual <a href = vnd.unilang:lust.html>lust</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Rude or coarse in manner.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sexually aroused</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>horny</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">toey</span>; see also Thesaurus:<a href = vnd.unilang:randy.html>randy</a></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">coarse</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">rude</span></li></ul>

***rangeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rangeren.html>rangeren</a> (100777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">ranger</i>. The railway sense may derive from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">rangieren</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rangeren.html>rangeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rail transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shunt, to <a href = vnd.unilang:marshal.html>marshal</a> <span class="defdate">[from late 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1872</b>, Jérome Alexandre Sillem, "Bibliographisch album", <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gids.html>Gids</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>Vol</a>. 36, page 348.

***ranja.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ranja.html>ranja</a> (67862)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Genericised trademark, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oranje.html>oranje</a></i> or a related word. The trademarked name <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> coined specifically for an orange-based cordial.
</p>
